\DoxyCodeLine{01461\ \textcolor{comment}{switch\ to\ native\ little-\/endian\ format\ for\ *all*\ arrays\ passed\ in\ and\ out\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01462\ \textcolor{comment}{public\ API.\ This\ includes\ public\ and\ private\ keys,\ shared\ secrets,\ signatures}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01465\ \textcolor{comment}{will\ *only*\ work\ on\ native\ little-\/endian\ processors\ and\ it\ will\ treat\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01466\ \textcolor{comment}{uint8\_t\ arrays\ passed\ into\ the\ public\ API\ as\ word\ arrays,\ therefore\ requiring}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01467\ \textcolor{comment}{the\ provided\ byte\ arrays\ to\ be\ word\ aligned\ on\ architectures\ that\ do\ not\ support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01468\ \textcolor{comment}{unaligned\ accesses.\ IMPORTANT:\ Keys\ and\ signatures\ generated\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01469\ \textcolor{comment}{MG\_UECC\_VLI\_NATIVE\_LITTLE\_ENDIAN=1\ are\ incompatible\ with\ keys\ and\ signatures}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01470\ \textcolor{comment}{generated\ with\ MG\_UECC\_VLI\_NATIVE\_LITTLE\_ENDIAN=0;\ all\ parties\ must\ use\ the\ same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01471\ \textcolor{comment}{endianness.\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01520\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01521\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01522\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ MG\_UECC\_RNG\_Function\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01523\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ RNG\ function\ should\ fill\ 'size'\ random\ bytes\ into\ 'dest'.\ It\ should\ return\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01524\ \textcolor{comment}{if\ 'dest'\ was\ filled\ with\ random\ data,\ or\ 0\ if\ the\ random\ data\ could\ not\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01525\ \textcolor{comment}{generated.\ The\ filled-\/in\ values\ should\ be\ either\ truly\ random,\ or\ from\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01526\ \textcolor{comment}{cryptographically-\/secure\ PRNG.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01527\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01528\ \textcolor{comment}{A\ correctly\ functioning\ RNG\ function\ must\ be\ set\ (using\ mg\_uecc\_set\_rng())}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01529\ \textcolor{comment}{before\ calling\ mg\_uecc\_make\_key()\ or\ mg\_uecc\_sign().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01530\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01531\ \textcolor{comment}{Setting\ a\ correctly\ functioning\ RNG\ function\ improves\ the\ resistance\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01532\ \textcolor{comment}{side-\/channel\ attacks\ for\ mg\_uecc\_shared\_secret()\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01533\ \textcolor{comment}{mg\_uecc\_sign\_deterministic().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01534\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01535\ \textcolor{comment}{A\ correct\ RNG\ function\ is\ set\ by\ default\ when\ building\ for\ Windows,\ Linux,\ or\ OS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01536\ \textcolor{comment}{X.\ If\ you\ are\ building\ on\ another\ POSIX-\/compliant\ system\ that\ supports}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01537\ \textcolor{comment}{/dev/random\ or\ /dev/urandom,\ you\ can\ define\ MG\_UECC\_POSIX\ to\ use\ the\ predefined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01538\ \textcolor{comment}{RNG.\ For\ embedded\ platforms\ there\ is\ no\ predefined\ RNG\ function;\ you\ must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01539\ \textcolor{comment}{provide\ your\ own.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01540\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01693\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ MG\_UECC\_HashContext\ structure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01694\ \textcolor{comment}{This\ is\ used\ to\ pass\ in\ an\ arbitrary\ hash\ function\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01695\ \textcolor{comment}{mg\_uecc\_sign\_deterministic().\ The\ structure\ will\ be\ used\ for\ multiple\ hash}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01696\ \textcolor{comment}{computations;\ each\ time\ a\ new\ hash\ is\ computed,\ init\_hash()\ will\ be\ called,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01697\ \textcolor{comment}{followed\ by\ one\ or\ more\ calls\ to\ update\_hash(),\ and\ finally\ a\ call\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01698\ \textcolor{comment}{finish\_hash()\ to\ produce\ the\ resulting\ hash.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01699\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01700\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ intention\ is\ that\ you\ will\ create\ a\ structure\ that\ includes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01701\ \textcolor{comment}{MG\_UECC\_HashContext\ followed\ by\ any\ hash-\/specific\ data.\ For\ example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01702\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01710\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ SHA256\_Init(\&context-\/>ctx);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01711\ \textcolor{comment}{\}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01723\ \textcolor{comment}{\}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01724\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01728\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ SHA256\_HashContext\ ctx\ =\ \{\{\&init\_SHA256,\ \&update\_SHA256,\ \&finish\_SHA256,\ 64,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01729\ \textcolor{comment}{32,\ tmp\}\};\ mg\_uecc\_sign\_deterministic(key,\ message\_hash,\ \&ctx.uECC,\ signature);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01730\ \textcolor{comment}{\}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01731\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01745\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01746\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ mg\_uecc\_sign\_deterministic()\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01747\ \textcolor{comment}{Generate\ an\ ECDSA\ signature\ for\ a\ given\ hash\ value,\ using\ a\ deterministic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01748\ \textcolor{comment}{algorithm\ (see\ RFC\ 6979).\ You\ do\ not\ need\ to\ set\ the\ RNG\ using\ mg\_uecc\_set\_rng()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01749\ \textcolor{comment}{before\ calling\ this\ function;\ however,\ if\ the\ RNG\ is\ defined\ it\ will\ improve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01750\ \textcolor{comment}{resistance\ to\ side-\/channel\ attacks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01751\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02092\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02093\ \textcolor{comment}{\ This\ library\ implements\ RFC\ 8439\ a.k.a.\ ChaCha20-\/Poly1305\ AEAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02094\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02095\ \textcolor{comment}{\ You\ can\ use\ this\ library\ to\ avoid\ attackers\ mutating\ or\ reusing\ your}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02098\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02124\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02125\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ Encrypt/Seal\ plain\ text\ bytes\ into\ a\ cipher\ text\ that\ can\ only\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02126\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ decrypted\ by\ knowing\ the\ key,\ nonce\ and\ associated\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02127\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ input:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ key:\ RFC\_8439\_KEY\_SIZE\ bytes\ that\ all\ parties\ have\ agreed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02130\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ upon\ beforehand}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02131\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ nonce:\ RFC\_8439\_NONCE\_SIZE\ bytes\ that\ should\ never\ be\ repeated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02132\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ for\ the\ same\ key.\ A\ counter\ or\ a\ pseudo-\/random\ value\ are\ fine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02133\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ ad:\ associated\ data\ to\ include\ with\ calculating\ the\ tag\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02134\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ cipher\ text.\ Can\ be\ null\ for\ empty.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02135\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ plain\_text:\ data\ to\ be\ encrypted,\ pointer\ +\ size\ should\ not\ overlap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02136\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ with\ cipher\_text\ pointer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02137\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02138\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ output:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02139\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ cipher\_text:\ encrypted\ plain\_text\ with\ a\ tag\ appended.\ Make\ sure\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02140\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ allocate\ at\ least\ plain\_text\_size\ +\ RFC\_8439\_TAG\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02141\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02142\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ returns:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02143\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ size\ of\ bytes\ written\ to\ cipher\_text,\ can\ be\ -\/1\ if\ overlapping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02144\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ pointers\ are\ passed\ for\ plain\_text\ and\ cipher\_text}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02145\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
